Note (1): Reference, quasar classification --
    DR7Q       = SDSS DR7; Schneider et al. (2010AJ....139.2360S);
    DR14Q      = SDSS DR14; Paris et al. (2018A&A...613A..51P);
    ELQS       = Extremely Luminous Quasar Survey; Schindler et al. (2017ApJ...851...13S);
    MQ         = Million Quasar Catalog, version 5.7b; Flesch (2015PASA...32...10F);
    PS-ELQS    = this work;
    other_qsos = Yang et al. (in preparation).
Note (2): Absolute magnitude at 1450A calculated using the k-correction determined for this work.
Note (3): The distance values are often 0 or otherwise extremely small,
    because the positions match to numerical accuracy.
Note (4): GALEX uncertainties of -999. indicate the GALEX magnitude is an upper limit.
Note (5): A flag indicating the most probable AllWISE ROSAT 2RXS cross-match
    with 1. This is the case for all matched objects.
Note (6): A flag indicating the most probable AllWISE XMMSL2 cross-match
    with 1. This is the case for all matched objects
